<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH600-23f228db--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9d7edec46b594839bd6023945993baa7"><span data-offset-key="9d7edec46b594839bd6023945993baa7:0">The Zen of Python</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="549a1f5ede2140138ea197be8c8795a3"><span data-offset-key="549a1f5ede2140138ea197be8c8795a3:0">From the </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0020/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a402ebfd09c7427b8215db615d2868e2"><span data-offset-key="a402ebfd09c7427b8215db615d2868e2:0">PEP 20 -- The Zen of Python</span></span></a><span data-key="29cee66f5b5f456e9ff5a9969dea66cd"><span data-offset-key="29cee66f5b5f456e9ff5a9969dea66cd:0">:</span></span></span>

> <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d1d1d499d794432d8bdd2ed1dd98bd03"><span data-offset-key="d1d1d499d794432d8bdd2ed1dd98bd03:0">Long time Pythoneer Tim Peters succinctly channels the BDFL's guiding principles for Python's design into 20 aphorisms, only 19 of which have been written down.</span></span></span>

    >>> import thisThe Zen of Python, by Tim Peters​Beautiful is better than ugly.Explicit is better than implicit.Simple is better than complex.Complex is better than complicated.Flat is better than nested.Sparse is better than dense.Readability counts.Special cases aren't special enough to break the rules.Although practicality beats purity.Errors should never pass silently.Unless explicitly silenced.In the face of ambiguity, refuse the temptation to guess.There should be one-- and preferably only one --obvious way to do it.Although that way may not be obvious at first unless you're Dutch.Now is better than never.Although never is often better than *right* now.If the implementation is hard to explain, it's a bad idea.If the implementation is easy to explain, it may be a good idea.Namespaces are one honking great idea -- let's do more of those!

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9800de8b6e4641089c8f4142bef0080e"><span data-offset-key="9800de8b6e4641089c8f4142bef0080e:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c755ea4727454c6ab52c84d1355f617b"><span data-offset-key="c755ea4727454c6ab52c84d1355f617b:0">String Concatenation and Replication</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="33644e70b0ee4b2caedcacf0a77e3fa2"><span data-offset-key="33644e70b0ee4b2caedcacf0a77e3fa2:0">String concatenation:</span></span></span>

    >>> 'Alice' 'Bob''AliceBob'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c8461723cb4d4965bddb4d7c1b364994"><span data-offset-key="c8461723cb4d4965bddb4d7c1b364994:0">Note: Avoid </span><span data-offset-key="c8461723cb4d4965bddb4d7c1b364994:1">`+`</span><span data-offset-key="c8461723cb4d4965bddb4d7c1b364994:2"> operator for string concatenation. Prefer string formatting.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a9be31cf4e5a4bf482b9ad55278140ab"><span data-offset-key="a9be31cf4e5a4bf482b9ad55278140ab:0">String Replication:</span></span></span>

    >>> 'Alice' * 5'AliceAliceAliceAliceAlice'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f53e9d243464446593774b960f009153"><span data-offset-key="f53e9d243464446593774b960f009153:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="69fe9884feb042c1b887a36af7bbdb8c"><span data-offset-key="69fe9884feb042c1b887a36af7bbdb8c:0">Variables</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b012fc5b375f473c86bf6f9a8b7391c5"><span data-offset-key="b012fc5b375f473c86bf6f9a8b7391c5:0">You can name a variable anything as long as it obeys the following rules:</span></span></span>

1.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7bcbfd7827294d668347f715d0b05c08"><span data-offset-key="7bcbfd7827294d668347f715d0b05c08:0">It can be only one word.</span></span></span>

2.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d4ef6f3623964574983646b313d3c302"><span data-offset-key="d4ef6f3623964574983646b313d3c302:0">It can use only letters, numbers, and the underscore (</span><span data-offset-key="d4ef6f3623964574983646b313d3c302:1">`_`</span><span data-offset-key="d4ef6f3623964574983646b313d3c302:2">) character.</span></span></span>

3.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="016096b9b9584f24aa48ea1971c539ed"><span data-offset-key="016096b9b9584f24aa48ea1971c539ed:0">It can’t begin with a number.</span></span></span>

4.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a0afc6f882174c829c259e206b5f8a1a"><span data-offset-key="a0afc6f882174c829c259e206b5f8a1a:0">Variable name starting with an underscore (</span><span data-offset-key="a0afc6f882174c829c259e206b5f8a1a:1">`_`</span><span data-offset-key="a0afc6f882174c829c259e206b5f8a1a:2">) are considered as "unuseful\`.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a8c430ad266e401faf4bce7c81785a94"><span data-offset-key="a8c430ad266e401faf4bce7c81785a94:0">Example:</span></span></span>

    >>> spam = 'Hello'>>> spam'Hello'

    >>> _spam = 'Hello'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7d4d9c1b213c4b59a25c568729b507a5"><span data-offset-key="7d4d9c1b213c4b59a25c568729b507a5:0">`_spam`</span><span data-offset-key="7d4d9c1b213c4b59a25c568729b507a5:1"> should not be used again in the code.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2ff795f8cff945d3ae0454d4d0341ad7"><span data-offset-key="2ff795f8cff945d3ae0454d4d0341ad7:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e66401f669284da8997518d31fbc1751"><span data-offset-key="e66401f669284da8997518d31fbc1751:0">Comments</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5f051557416b40a7a8333d886b4413c4"><span data-offset-key="5f051557416b40a7a8333d886b4413c4:0">Inline comment:</span></span></span>

    # This is a comment

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9d04890329824b14b532b6bda7c3f2fc"><span data-offset-key="9d04890329824b14b532b6bda7c3f2fc:0">Multiline comment:</span></span></span>

    # This is a# multiline comment

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5c925e5302e64f658495b3fd087f3742"><span data-offset-key="5c925e5302e64f658495b3fd087f3742:0">Code with a comment:</span></span></span>

    a = 1  # initialization

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c9994f5cfc4a4dd1bdc580734b6aa474"><span data-offset-key="c9994f5cfc4a4dd1bdc580734b6aa474:0">Please note the two spaces in front of the comment.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0505f168650f4582a3cb45391d118f02"><span data-offset-key="0505f168650f4582a3cb45391d118f02:0">Function docstring:</span></span></span>

    def foo():    """    This is a function docstring    You can also use:    ''' Function Docstring '''    """

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f89397e9ae8440358551be6fbcb25d85"><span data-offset-key="f89397e9ae8440358551be6fbcb25d85:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c85985a8228b430d93becdc4c8f3ea66"><span data-offset-key="c85985a8228b430d93becdc4c8f3ea66:0">The print() Function</span></span></span>

    >>> print('Hello world!')Hello world!

    >>> a = 1>>> print('Hello world!', a)Hello world! 1

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="33bad496815a469db4e2edd4c9b3a215"><span data-offset-key="33bad496815a469db4e2edd4c9b3a215:0">The input() Function</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e4e47a99eb8f454693baebbbd8fe06c8"><span data-offset-key="e4e47a99eb8f454693baebbbd8fe06c8:0">Example Code:</span></span></span>

    >>> print('What is your name?')   # ask for their name>>> myName = input()>>> print('It is good to meet you, {}'.format(myName))What is your name?AlIt is good to meet you, Al

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="64d6bf297e4d4c77acd6c1e648eedf1d"><span data-offset-key="64d6bf297e4d4c77acd6c1e648eedf1d:0">The len() Function</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="183ebc5d09b34981bdf26dbf43c5b8cf"><span data-offset-key="183ebc5d09b34981bdf26dbf43c5b8cf:0">Evaluates to the integer value of the number of characters in a string:</span></span></span>

    >>> len('hello')5

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="94b553ef57254d2a854a637c54ee8a08"><span data-offset-key="94b553ef57254d2a854a637c54ee8a08:0">Note: test of emptiness of strings, lists, dictionary, etc, should </span><span data-offset-key="94b553ef57254d2a854a637c54ee8a08:1">**not**</span><span data-offset-key="94b553ef57254d2a854a637c54ee8a08:2"> use len, but prefer direct boolean evaluation.</span></span></span>

    >>> a = [1, 2, 3]>>> if a:>>>     print("the list is not empty!")

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="178f6904841c4667b3739069f41e84a8"><span data-offset-key="178f6904841c4667b3739069f41e84a8:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="15bf7c1ee8a54780b8230e0a695a8ece"><span data-offset-key="15bf7c1ee8a54780b8230e0a695a8ece:0">The str(), int(), and float() Functions</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9c19c41ebae14255b82c7624aafccd3e"><span data-offset-key="9c19c41ebae14255b82c7624aafccd3e:0">Integer to String or Float:</span></span></span>

    >>> str(29)'29'

    >>> print('I am {} years old.'.format(str(29)))I am 29 years old.

    >>> str(-3.14)'-3.14'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2c23a432ec1f4dc3a9cff06ef4240d5c"><span data-offset-key="2c23a432ec1f4dc3a9cff06ef4240d5c:0">Float to Integer:</span></span></span>

    >>> int(7.7)7

    >>> int(7.7) + 18

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="23b768d9829049698c9ccb03ae61b652"><span data-offset-key="23b768d9829049698c9ccb03ae61b652:0">Comparison Operators</span></span></span>

data-slate-leaf="true">&gt;=</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="75196182bd434e0a99b0ee17f0135f8a"><span data-offset-key="75196182bd434e0a99b0ee17f0135f8a:0">Greater than or Equal to</span></span></span></p></td></tr></tbody></table>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1dee0776a2834b0a90c2f91a49b69f12"><span data-offset-key="1dee0776a2834b0a90c2f91a49b69f12:0">These operators evaluate to True or False depending on the values you give them.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="078a0906ebd0482a8abeccc900e6e83c"><span data-offset-key="078a0906ebd0482a8abeccc900e6e83c:0">Examples:</span></span></span>

    >>> 42 == 42True

    >>> 40 == 42False

    >>> 'hello' == 'hello'True

    >>> 'hello' == 'Hello'False

    >>> 'dog' != 'cat'True

    >>> 42 == 42.0True

    >>> 42 == '42'False

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b73a9272a8204e578b8565060153901a"><span data-offset-key="b73a9272a8204e578b8565060153901a:0">Boolean evaluation</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c82717f3e65c426c8f6f6116281f3f85"><span data-offset-key="c82717f3e65c426c8f6f6116281f3f85:0">Never use </span><span data-offset-key="c82717f3e65c426c8f6f6116281f3f85:1">`==`</span><span data-offset-key="c82717f3e65c426c8f6f6116281f3f85:2"> or </span><span data-offset-key="c82717f3e65c426c8f6f6116281f3f85:3">`!=`</span><span data-offset-key="c82717f3e65c426c8f6f6116281f3f85:4"> operator to evaluate boolean operation. Use the </span><span data-offset-key="c82717f3e65c426c8f6f6116281f3f85:5">`is`</span><span data-offset-key="c82717f3e65c426c8f6f6116281f3f85:6"> or </span><span data-offset-key="c82717f3e65c426c8f6f6116281f3f85:7">`is not`</span><span data-offset-key="c82717f3e65c426c8f6f6116281f3f85:8"> operators, or use implicit boolean evaluation.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="69e93bf3066646858aa92bdaf51518fc"><span data-offset-key="69e93bf3066646858aa92bdaf51518fc:0">NO (even if they are valid Python):</span></span></span>

    >>> True == TrueTrue

    >>> True != FalseTrue

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="23b661bed9674ba8a3e3d3a878891613"><span data-offset-key="23b661bed9674ba8a3e3d3a878891613:0">YES (even if they are valid Python):</span></span></span>

    >>> True is TrueTrue

    >>> True is not FalseTrue

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d47238ed1d51420e9649fb1b3003b87d"><span data-offset-key="d47238ed1d51420e9649fb1b3003b87d:0">These statements are equivalent:</span></span></span>

    >>> if a is True:>>>    pass>>> if a is not False:>>>    pass>>> if a:>>>    pass

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3963ac1f2882470dabf68f6e3c9b21db"><span data-offset-key="3963ac1f2882470dabf68f6e3c9b21db:0">And these as well:</span></span></span>

    >>> if a is False:>>>    pass>>> if a is not True:>>>    pass>>> if not a:>>>    pass

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7514b3f094ca4578a1bb23898b78a519"><span data-offset-key="7514b3f094ca4578a1bb23898b78a519:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b642ee7c1190466ab020a0bb506ecf61"><span data-offset-key="b642ee7c1190466ab020a0bb506ecf61:0">Boolean Operators</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="aca528e9ef6b4520b0576239310a1e32"><span data-offset-key="aca528e9ef6b4520b0576239310a1e32:0">There are three Boolean operators: and, or, and not.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a3d94672c715453ba1bcb5ce80f08846"><span data-offset-key="a3d94672c715453ba1bcb5ce80f08846:0">The </span><span data-offset-key="a3d94672c715453ba1bcb5ce80f08846:1">*and*</span><span data-offset-key="a3d94672c715453ba1bcb5ce80f08846:2"> Operator’s </span><span data-offset-key="a3d94672c715453ba1bcb5ce80f08846:3">*Truth*</span><span data-offset-key="a3d94672c715453ba1bcb5ce80f08846:4"> Table:</span></span></span>

<table><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><tbody><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--UIH400-4e41e82a--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b7eea03305bb4de793309822c01c1586"><span data-offset-key="b7eea03305bb4de793309822c01c1586:0">Expression</span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span <span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ba80353a79dc4f65bc962d75ffc35867"><span data-offset-key="ba80353a79dc4f65bc962d75ffc35867:0">Mixing Boolean and Comparison Operators</span></span></span>

    >>> (4 < 5) and (5 < 6)True

    >>> (4 < 5) and (9 < 6)False

    >>> (1 == 2) or (2 == 2)True

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4437f31021c44ddeacb0a526b3b10f7b"><span data-offset-key="4437f31021c44ddeacb0a526b3b10f7b:0">You can also use multiple Boolean operators in an expression, along with the comparison operators:</span></span></span>

    >>> 2 + 2 == 4 and not 2 + 2 == 5 and 2 * 2 == 2 + 2True

    name = 'Bob'age = 5if name == 'Alice':    print('Hi, Alice.')elif age < 12:    print('You are not Alice, kiddo.')

    spam = 0while spam < 5:    print('Hello, world.')    spam = spam + 1

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d0b8cf3d0345498cb741cd23677dda71"><span data-offset-key="d0b8cf3d0345498cb741cd23677dda71:0">break Statements</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3a20fdf030a149769037feac09562983"><span data-offset-key="3a20fdf030a149769037feac09562983:0">If the execution reaches a break statement, it immediately exits the while loop’s clause:</span></span></span>

    while True:    print('Please type your name.')    name = input()    if name == 'your name':        breakprint('Thank you!')

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="aa8d31f39630403d85cbd52298244a24"><span data-offset-key="aa8d31f39630403d85cbd52298244a24:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1a200cf481f8435399321c40341d3e0a"><span data-offset-key="1a200cf481f8435399321c40341d3e0a:0">continue Statements</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="37daef796eb44f9498c1134649b0130f"><span data-offset-key="37daef796eb44f9498c1134649b0130f:0">When the program execution reaches a continue statement, the program execution immediately jumps back to the start of the loop.</span></span></span>

    while True:    print('Who are you?')    name = input()    if name != 'Joe':        continue    print('Hello, Joe. What is the password? (It is a fish.)')    password = input()    if password == 'swordfish':        breakprint('Access granted.')

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a9b324e2bc9b4291b95b299ea1c09e8b"><span data-offset-key="a9b324e2bc9b4291b95b299ea1c09e8b:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3177e20bbc3b4a1ba49c6af44852f38d"><span data-offset-key="3177e20bbc3b4a1ba49c6af44852f38d:0">for Loops and the range() Function</span></span></span>

    >>> print('My name is')>>> for i in range(5):>>>     print('Jimmy Five Times ({})'.format(str(i)))My name isJimmy Five Times (0)Jimmy Five Times (1)Jimmy Five Times (2)Jimmy Five Times (3)Jimmy Five Times (4)

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ae032e102fb14feb958d23b485781c79"><span data-offset-key="ae032e102fb14feb958d23b485781c79:0">The </span><span data-offset-key="ae032e102fb14feb958d23b485781c79:1">*range()*</span><span data-offset-key="ae032e102fb14feb958d23b485781c79:2"> function can also be called with three arguments. The first two arguments will be the start and stop values, and the third will be the step argument. The step is the amount that the variable is increased by after each iteration.</span></span></span>

    >>> for i in range(0, 10, 2):>>>    print(i)02468

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="cc579f6eca154fdbba01d2a238c0bbd8"><span data-offset-key="cc579f6eca154fdbba01d2a238c0bbd8:0">You can even use a negative number for the step argument to make the for loop count down instead of up.</span></span></span>

    >>> for i in range(5, -1, -1):>>>     print(i)543210

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0de128951d6242728f00c62052013c3f"><span data-offset-key="0de128951d6242728f00c62052013c3f:0">For else statement</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7d1799522fa04be9a39a700e80febd01"><span data-offset-key="7d1799522fa04be9a39a700e80febd01:0">This allows to specify a statement to execute in case of the full loop has been executed. Only useful when a </span><span data-offset-key="7d1799522fa04be9a39a700e80febd01:1">`break`</span><span data-offset-key="7d1799522fa04be9a39a700e80febd01:2"> condition can occur in the loop:</span></span></span>

    >>> for i in [1, 2, 3, 4, 5]:>>>    if i == 3:>>>        break>>> else:>>>    print("only executed when no item of the list is equal to 3")

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6598ae6f809443ea9a08536d406e1e04"><span data-offset-key="6598ae6f809443ea9a08536d406e1e04:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

    import randomfor i in range(5):    print(random.randint(1, 10))

    import random, sys, os, math

    from random import *

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d5f8e13658c74190b5e27c09b18167b1"><span data-offset-key="d5f8e13658c74190b5e27c09b18167b1:0">Ending a Program Early with sys.exit()</span></span></span>

    import sys​while True:    print('Type exit to exit.')    response = input()    if response == 'exit':        sys.exit()    print('You typed {}.'.format(response))

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a92d99e84b9147a4a49e5db9b3579ea8"><span data-offset-key="a92d99e84b9147a4a49e5db9b3579ea8:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH600-23f228db--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="97ae553dc146422d9e884be8f28b40aa"><span data-offset-key="97ae553dc146422d9e884be8f28b40aa:0">Functions</span></span></span>

    >>> def hello(name):>>>     print('Hello {}'.format(name))>>>>>> hello('Alice')>>> hello('Bob')Hello AliceHello Bob

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8d745f0007ce489eb2da6274098800b5"><span data-offset-key="8d745f0007ce489eb2da6274098800b5:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d9b5d78820d545b3bf5dfcc871031418"><span data-offset-key="d9b5d78820d545b3bf5dfcc871031418:0">Return Values and return Statements</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="244b9f7b37a54a09985265022135bd1b"><span data-offset-key="244b9f7b37a54a09985265022135bd1b:0">When creating a function using the def statement, you can specify what the return value should be with a return statement. A return statement consists of the following:</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="94212a610c40427dae6d26843528ab75"><span data-offset-key="94212a610c40427dae6d26843528ab75:0">The return keyword.</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a914947c391d4748b28f9c85465ddf73"><span data-offset-key="a914947c391d4748b28f9c85465ddf73:0">The value or expression that the function should return.</span></span></span>

    import randomdef getAnswer(answerNumber):    if answerNumber == 1:        return 'It is certain'    elif answerNumber == 2:        return 'It is decidedly so'    elif answerNumber == 3:        return 'Yes'    elif answerNumber == 4:        return 'Reply hazy try again'    elif answerNumber == 5:        return 'Ask again later'    elif answerNumber == 6:        return 'Concentrate and ask again'    elif answerNumber == 7:        return 'My reply is no'    elif answerNumber == 8:        return 'Outlook not so good'    elif answerNumber == 9:        return 'Very doubtful'​r = random.randint(1, 9)fortune = getAnswer(r)print(fortune)

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b1254727bdb9458f8a4a3ae7f35f2acd"><span data-offset-key="b1254727bdb9458f8a4a3ae7f35f2acd:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4c3d576cf9544cfbbe0a59932ce64bb5"><span data-offset-key="4c3d576cf9544cfbbe0a59932ce64bb5:0">The None Value</span></span></span>

    >>> spam = print('Hello!')Hello!

    >>> spam is NoneTrue

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a648bed72c494980bb5173bfb411d1dd"><span data-offset-key="a648bed72c494980bb5173bfb411d1dd:0">Note: never compare to </span><span data-offset-key="a648bed72c494980bb5173bfb411d1dd:1">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="a648bed72c494980bb5173bfb411d1dd:2"> with the </span><span data-offset-key="a648bed72c494980bb5173bfb411d1dd:3">`==`</span><span data-offset-key="a648bed72c494980bb5173bfb411d1dd:4"> operator. Always use </span><span data-offset-key="a648bed72c494980bb5173bfb411d1dd:5">`is`</span><span data-offset-key="a648bed72c494980bb5173bfb411d1dd:6">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7bc6a9ef4a684fc58b3e088a3ffc2768"><span data-offset-key="7bc6a9ef4a684fc58b3e088a3ffc2768:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="01eeeb2ece07448db705fa5418c0186e"><span data-offset-key="01eeeb2ece07448db705fa5418c0186e:0">Keyword Arguments and print()</span></span></span>

    >>> print('Hello', end='')>>> print('World')HelloWorld

    >>> print('cats', 'dogs', 'mice')cats dogs mice

    >>> print('cats', 'dogs', 'mice', sep=',')cats,dogs,mice

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3edc6739bdb5463fa8d379fb3baaf0d7"><span data-offset-key="3edc6739bdb5463fa8d379fb3baaf0d7:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="10a36831e9874406be55478bb5037056"><span data-offset-key="10a36831e9874406be55478bb5037056:0">Local and Global Scope</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="beb3101a4f124e39956a6c00e6fa3054"><span data-offset-key="beb3101a4f124e39956a6c00e6fa3054:0">Code in the global scope cannot use any local variables.</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1e98dc2e49a141baa29a32262e314b5d"><span data-offset-key="1e98dc2e49a141baa29a32262e314b5d:0">However, a local scope can access global variables.</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="bf84b8651b70438ea9b6b8ac5bc34474"><span data-offset-key="bf84b8651b70438ea9b6b8ac5bc34474:0">Code in a function’s local scope cannot use variables in any other local scope.</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7d6c248965cf4c0d9de15f72464335f4"><span data-offset-key="7d6c248965cf4c0d9de15f72464335f4:0">You can use the same name for different variables if they are in different scopes. That is, there can be a local variable named spam and a global variable also named spam.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0145b013b9f5476dab14e2e93702085b"><span data-offset-key="0145b013b9f5476dab14e2e93702085b:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3ce0071003254464b41e155d77e97279"><span data-offset-key="3ce0071003254464b41e155d77e97279:0">The global Statement</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a7b75e4abae248e5842f5c0ea548ce94"><span data-offset-key="a7b75e4abae248e5842f5c0ea548ce94:0">If you need to modify a global variable from within a function, use the global statement:</span></span></span>

    >>> def spam():>>>     global eggs>>>     eggs = 'spam'>>>>>> eggs = 'global'>>> spam()>>> print(eggs)spam

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1a7ce1daaea74b848436b5b7cf92f218"><span data-offset-key="1a7ce1daaea74b848436b5b7cf92f218:0">There are four rules to tell whether a variable is in a local scope or global scope:</span></span></span>

1.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b89890234d394b39a97ba58213758c73"><span data-offset-key="b89890234d394b39a97ba58213758c73:0">If a variable is being used in the global scope (that is, outside of all functions), then it is always a global variable.</span></span></span>

2.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4d4b3838b9b044a1bfd4e5057eb79371"><span data-offset-key="4d4b3838b9b044a1bfd4e5057eb79371:0">If there is a global statement for that variable in a function, it is a global variable.</span></span></span>

3.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7345ef1482ee4ec9867856961d402bf8"><span data-offset-key="7345ef1482ee4ec9867856961d402bf8:0">Otherwise, if the variable is used in an assignment statement in the function, it is a local variable.</span></span></span>

4.  <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="cc5a775f1b2c42eabfd698292c8e3a36"><span data-offset-key="cc5a775f1b2c42eabfd698292c8e3a36:0">But if the variable is not used in an assignment statement, it is a global variable.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9b4226b9c60b4a28af2e41d316ace229"><span data-offset-key="9b4226b9c60b4a28af2e41d316ace229:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH600-23f228db--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="43ca0a147b3a4a1aa973bcd517995cae"><span data-offset-key="43ca0a147b3a4a1aa973bcd517995cae:0">Exception Handling</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6d7d2662bccc4fb399f10781c429341c"><span data-offset-key="6d7d2662bccc4fb399f10781c429341c:0">Basic exception handling</span></span></span>

    >>> def spam(divideBy):>>>     try:>>>         return 42 / divideBy>>>     except ZeroDivisionError as e:>>>         print('Error: Invalid argument: {}'.format(e))>>>>>> print(spam(2))>>> print(spam(12))>>> print(spam(0))>>> print(spam(1))21.03.5Error: Invalid argument: division by zeroNone42.0

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c0495d16073d4ddbb6fb366d2ded3c07"><span data-offset-key="c0495d16073d4ddbb6fb366d2ded3c07:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2ca520f34be74ac0ad193be00c9b5202"><span data-offset-key="2ca520f34be74ac0ad193be00c9b5202:0">Final code in exception handling</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6099dd04cd7b43a9990aa5c849d9b4be"><span data-offset-key="6099dd04cd7b43a9990aa5c849d9b4be:0">Code inside the </span><span data-offset-key="6099dd04cd7b43a9990aa5c849d9b4be:1">`finally`</span><span data-offset-key="6099dd04cd7b43a9990aa5c849d9b4be:2"> section is always executed, no matter if an exception has been raised or not, and even if an exception is not caught.</span></span></span>

    >>> def spam(divideBy):>>>     try:>>>         return 42 / divideBy>>>     except ZeroDivisionError as e:>>>         print('Error: Invalid argument: {}'.format(e))>>>     finally:>>>         print("-- division finished --")>>> print(spam(2))-- division finished --21.0>>> print(spam(12))-- division finished --3.5>>> print(spam(0))Error: Invalid Argument division by zero-- division finished --None>>> print(spam(1))-- division finished --42.0

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="89254fd5ff1f4adfa59b7cf56a42f54c"><span data-offset-key="89254fd5ff1f4adfa59b7cf56a42f54c:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH600-23f228db--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="dcf033578c504d908f22d905228e4f2d"><span data-offset-key="dcf033578c504d908f22d905228e4f2d:0">Lists</span></span></span>

    >>> spam = ['cat', 'bat', 'rat', 'elephant']​>>> spam['cat', 'bat', 'rat', 'elephant']

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a26c4a3a8c5a4188b8d54730712396c7"><span data-offset-key="a26c4a3a8c5a4188b8d54730712396c7:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8531a613c4f84d97b598b4b37847bfd1"><span data-offset-key="8531a613c4f84d97b598b4b37847bfd1:0">Getting Individual Values in a List with Indexes</span></span></span>

    >>> spam = ['cat', 'bat', 'rat', 'elephant']>>> spam[0]'cat'

    >>> spam[1]'bat'

    >>> spam[2]'rat'

    >>> spam[3]'elephant'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="58d2e8bb71f84f22af34296a30c6e43c"><span data-offset-key="58d2e8bb71f84f22af34296a30c6e43c:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9f0a4cd60db048049e09d2fbd6ab7d31"><span data-offset-key="9f0a4cd60db048049e09d2fbd6ab7d31:0">Negative Indexes</span></span></span>

    >>> spam = ['cat', 'bat', 'rat', 'elephant']>>> spam[-1]'elephant'

    >>> spam[-3]'bat'

    >>> 'The {} is afraid of the {}.'.format(spam[-1], spam[-3])'The elephant is afraid of the bat.'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1236ff7ea3204ea991d38bc0b7446fa4"><span data-offset-key="1236ff7ea3204ea991d38bc0b7446fa4:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b783835291ca4978b1fb50d2184f2357"><span data-offset-key="b783835291ca4978b1fb50d2184f2357:0">Getting Sublists with Slices</span></span></span>

    >>> spam = ['cat', 'bat', 'rat', 'elephant']>>> spam[0:4]['cat', 'bat', 'rat', 'elephant']

    >>> spam[1:3]['bat', 'rat']

    >>> spam[0:-1]['cat', 'bat', 'rat']

    >>> spam = ['cat', 'bat', 'rat', 'elephant']>>> spam[:2]['cat', 'bat']

    >>> spam[1:]['bat', 'rat', 'elephant']

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d71f57f87c054c549f7b19fe64873594"><span data-offset-key="d71f57f87c054c549f7b19fe64873594:0">Slicing the complete list will perform a copy:</span></span></span>

    >>> spam2 = spam[:]['cat', 'bat', 'rat', 'elephant']>>> spam.append('dog')>>> spam['cat', 'bat', 'rat', 'elephant', 'dog']>>> spam2['cat', 'bat', 'rat', 'elephant']

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7fdedaf45c4d4af19db5c8c6dbe5395d"><span data-offset-key="7fdedaf45c4d4af19db5c8c6dbe5395d:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a6985a918799459b97f5b35a46dfcf02"><span data-offset-key="a6985a918799459b97f5b35a46dfcf02:0">Getting a List’s Length with len()</span></span></span>

    >>> spam = ['cat', 'dog', 'moose']>>> len(spam)3

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d110ae9ce9e4432388f0974815b7804c"><span data-offset-key="d110ae9ce9e4432388f0974815b7804c:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2ce9ca51ff28439aac93940ab87f024a"><span data-offset-key="2ce9ca51ff28439aac93940ab87f024a:0">Changing Values in a List with Indexes</span></span></span>

    >>> spam = ['cat', 'bat', 'rat', 'elephant']>>> spam[1] = 'aardvark'​>>> spam['cat', 'aardvark', 'rat', 'elephant']​>>> spam[2] = spam[1]​>>> spam['cat', 'aardvark', 'aardvark', 'elephant']​>>> spam[-1] = 12345​>>> spam['cat', 'aardvark', 'aardvark', 12345]

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="01d2b9f1a01a4ce98b6768eddf2b8898"><span data-offset-key="01d2b9f1a01a4ce98b6768eddf2b8898:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ce3601b9990c4e74a965aaec33aedbd8"><span data-offset-key="ce3601b9990c4e74a965aaec33aedbd8:0">List Concatenation and List Replication</span></span></span>

    >>> [1, 2, 3] + ['A', 'B', 'C'][1, 2, 3, 'A', 'B', 'C']​>>> ['X', 'Y', 'Z'] * 3['X', 'Y', 'Z', 'X', 'Y', 'Z', 'X', 'Y', 'Z']​>>> spam = [1, 2, 3]​>>> spam = spam + ['A', 'B', 'C']​>>> spam[1, 2, 3, 'A', 'B', 'C']

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c16f995e94b447d7a5416c904cf7dbe1"><span data-offset-key="c16f995e94b447d7a5416c904cf7dbe1:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ae0832acb3814d4b8f74bf19d315c9ee"><span data-offset-key="ae0832acb3814d4b8f74bf19d315c9ee:0">Removing Values from Lists with del Statements</span></span></span>

    >>> spam = ['cat', 'bat', 'rat', 'elephant']>>> del spam[2]>>> spam['cat', 'bat', 'elephant']

    >>> del spam[2]>>> spam['cat', 'bat']

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="430910197ff34d6e8bff2dad94f5411e"><span data-offset-key="430910197ff34d6e8bff2dad94f5411e:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6978997b54f84fe5a6d608a851401b07"><span data-offset-key="6978997b54f84fe5a6d608a851401b07:0">Using for Loops with Lists</span></span></span>

    >>> supplies = ['pens', 'staplers', 'flame-throwers', 'binders']>>> for i, supply in enumerate(supplies):>>>     print('Index {} in supplies is: {}'.format(str(i), supply))Index 0 in supplies is: pensIndex 1 in supplies is: staplersIndex 2 in supplies is: flame-throwersIndex 3 in supplies is: binders

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e709bbce6087481bae450743fd920283"><span data-offset-key="e709bbce6087481bae450743fd920283:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d73814b5aba44f65b7736cfd93efbdde"><span data-offset-key="d73814b5aba44f65b7736cfd93efbdde:0">Looping Through Multiple Lists with zip()</span></span></span>

    >>> name = ['Pete', 'John', 'Elizabeth']>>> age = [6, 23, 44]>>> for n, a in zip(name, age):>>>     print('{} is {} years old'.format(n, a))Pete is 6 years oldJohn is 23 years oldElizabeth is 44 years old

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="01f9489080164b5a8891adf16fef1ce9"><span data-offset-key="01f9489080164b5a8891adf16fef1ce9:0">The in and not in Operators</span></span></span>

    >>> 'howdy' in ['hello', 'hi', 'howdy', 'heyas']True

    >>> spam = ['hello', 'hi', 'howdy', 'heyas']>>> 'cat' in spamFalse

    >>> 'howdy' not in spamFalse

    >>> 'cat' not in spamTrue

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1d445a246892468dbaa2307b8f8e3f71"><span data-offset-key="1d445a246892468dbaa2307b8f8e3f71:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a424bcd306a44a6b9a58af0e46e8df8e"><span data-offset-key="a424bcd306a44a6b9a58af0e46e8df8e:0">The Multiple Assignment Trick</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c176ff0887d2487da0742d351addbb75"><span data-offset-key="c176ff0887d2487da0742d351addbb75:0">The multiple assignment trick is a shortcut that lets you assign multiple variables with the values in a list in one line of code. So instead of doing this:</span></span></span>

    >>> cat = ['fat', 'orange', 'loud']​>>> size = cat[0]​>>> color = cat[1]​>>> disposition = cat[2]

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0cf970a684c74dc696463b9df640564f"><span data-offset-key="0cf970a684c74dc696463b9df640564f:0">You could type this line of code:</span></span></span>

    >>> cat = ['fat', 'orange', 'loud']​>>> size, color, disposition = cat

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="addc5c0e26114a798a49ba2a5a10cb2f"><span data-offset-key="addc5c0e26114a798a49ba2a5a10cb2f:0">The multiple assignment trick can also be used to swap the values in two variables:</span></span></span>

    >>> a, b = 'Alice', 'Bob'>>> a, b = b, a>>> print(a)'Bob'

    >>> print(b)'Alice'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5f4cd34f75f44f13bd847bcb3674521a"><span data-offset-key="5f4cd34f75f44f13bd847bcb3674521a:0">*Return to the Top*</span></span></span>

### 

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d6adb6c4fa964fd5aaad70c9dc479532"><span data-offset-key="d6adb6c4fa964fd5aaad70c9dc479532:0">Augmented Assignment Operators</span></span></span>

<table><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><tbody><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--UIH400-4e41e82a--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f0a5726131ce41a495f96356c18fa04f"><span data-offset-key="f0a5726131ce41a495f96356c18fa04f:0">Operator</span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--UIH400-4e41e82a--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2823dee533fb4ecdb3f21d169dd735d6"><span data-offset-key="2823dee533fb4ecdb3f21d169dd735d6:0">Equivalent</span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="even"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0553705942464e4fb911986c39fd7ee5"><span data-offset-key="0553705942464e4fb911986c39fd7ee5:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">spam += 1</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="06d24e5d25324db6989844fb30663e19"><span data-offset-key="06d24e5d25324db6989844fb30663e19:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">spam = spam + 1</code></span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b671fdeb279c4cdc9cd7a1823696cdf2"><span data-offset-key="b671fdeb279c4cdc9cd7a1823696cdf2:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">spam -= 1</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="040eb31a674a4ecca03b8aabad6cec1d"><span data-offset-key="040eb31a674a4ecca03b8aabad6cec1d:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">spam = spam - 1</code></span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="even"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f1bf353ec94e46b5af570192a3698420"><span data-offset-key="f1bf353ec94e46b5af570192a3698420:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">spam *= 1</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ab0978cc674e464098e5602837859d48"><span data-offset-key="ab0978cc674e464098e5602837859d48:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">spam = spam * 1</code></span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9b6e7357f6b64b9d8cf8161c41a57568"><span data-offset-key="9b6e7357f6b64b9d8cf8161c41a57568:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">spam /= 1</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="110e623a75df405886f68ab93d2244b3"><span data-offset-key="110e623a75df405886f68ab93d2244b3:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">spam = spam / 1</code></span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="even"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="dee51fda3afc40cc8dd444ff77e288e7"><span data-offset-key="dee51fda3afc40cc8dd444ff77e288e7:0"><code
